 - The first of the nine letters of the Navarna Mantra is Ain, which governs the planet Sun

 - The second letter is Hreen, which controls the planet Moon

 - The third letter is Klein, the fourth letter is Cha, the fifth letter is Mun, the sixth letter is Da, the seventh letter is, the eighth is v and the ninth is Cha, which controls the planets Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus, Saturn, Rahu and Ketu
